##### Generated SQL Query

```SQL
SELECT COUNT(*) AS ""COUNT(*)"" FROM (SELECT * FROM vax_data WHERE age_yrs = '89.0') AS t1;
```

#### Example 2

##### Input

```JSON
{
    ""query"": {
        ""question"": ""How many patients are 89.0 years old."",
        ""field_names"": [

			AND vax_type = 'VAX'
		UNION SELECT DISTINCT
			VAERS_ID
		FROM
			vaers_data
		WHERE
			vax_name = 'PNEUMO'
			AND vax_type = 'VAX'
	) AS t1;
```

##### Generated SQL

```sql
SELECT count(*) AS `count`
FROM `vax_data`.`vax_records` t1
WHERE (t1.`VAX_NAME` = 'Levothyroxine') AND (t1.`VAX_DOSE_SERIES` = '800 micrograms')
```
